l-container"\n          >\n              <article\n  data-uri="slate.com/_components/article/instances/ckfyqmref001bu9kwx9x8jz6v@published"\n  data-has-roadblock="false"\n  data-paywall-disabled="false"\n  data-rubric="politics"\n  class="article article--article"\n  itemscope\n  itemtype="http://schema.org/Article"\n>\n  <div itemprop="publisher" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Organization">\n    <meta itemprop="name" content="Slate" />\n    <div itemprop="logo" itemscope itemtype="https://www.schema.org/ImageObject">\n      <link itemprop="url" href="https://slate.com/media/sites/slate-com/icon.400x400.png">\n      <meta itemprop="width" content="400">\n      <meta itemprop="height" content="400">\n    </div>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class="article__fullbleed-header"></div>\n\n<header class="article__header">\n<div itemprop="image" itemscope itemtype="https://www.schema.org/ImageObject">\n          <meta itemprop="url" content="1200">\n          <meta itemprop="height" content="800">\n        </div>\n  <a\n  class="article__rubric"\n  href="/news-and-politics/politics"\n  \n>Politics</a>\n\n  <h1 itemprop="headline" class="article__hed" >Trump\xe2\x80\x99s Coronavirus Cover-Up Was All About Greed</h1>\n\n<h2 itemprop="alternativeHeadline"\n    class="article__dek" \n  >For two days, he deceived and endangered his supporters to get their money. Here\xe2\x80\x99s how he did it.</h2>\n<div class="article__meta">\n        <div class="article__byline" >\nBy\n      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">\n<span itemprop="name"><a href="/author/william-saletan">William Saletan</a></span></span>\n</div>\n  <time\n  itemprop="datePublished"\n  content="2020-10-07T02:12:35+00:00"\n  class="article__dateline"\n>\n  <span>Oct 06, 2020</span>10:12 PM</time>\n\n</div>\n    </header>\n  <div class="article__share-sidebar share-sidebar">\n      <ul\n  data-uri="slate.com/_components/social-share/instances/ckfyqmref0014u9kw0borx9mx@published"\n  class="social-share">\n  <li>\n    <a href="https://twitter.com/share?text=He%20did%20it%20for%20the%20money.&amp;via=slate&amp;url=https://slate.com/news-and-politics/2020/10/trump-coronavirus-cover-up-greed.html&utm_medium=social&utm_campaign=traffic&utm_content=twitter_share&utm_source=article"\n class="article__body">\n    <div class="article__content"  itemprop="mainEntityOfPage">\n          <figure\n  data-uri="slate.com/_components/image/instances/ckfyqmref0015u9kwsa9hne3q@published"\n  class="image image--center "\n  data-editable="imageInfo"\n>\n\n<div class="lazy-container" style="padding-bottom: 66.66666666666666%;">\n          <img class="image__src" data-normal="https://compote.slate.com/images/a06c32ef-452e-4880-ba9a-2b4eef367a02.jpeg?width&#x3D;780&amp;height&#x3D;520&amp;rect&#x3D;4622x3081&amp;offset&#x3D;309x172" alt="Trump giving a thumbs-up as he walks across a lawn" />\n          <noscript>\n            <img src="https://compote.slate.com/images/a06c32ef-452e-4880-ba9a-2b4eef367a02.jpeg?width&#x3D;780&amp;height&#x3D;520&amp;rect&#x3D;4622x3081&amp;offset&#x3D;309x172" alt="Trump giving a thumbs-up as he walks across a lawn" loading="lazy" />\n          </noscript>\n        </div>\n\n  <figcaption class="image__meta">\n<span class="image__caption">President Donald Trump walks to Marine One on Thursday in Washington.</span>\n<span class="image__credit">Drew Angerer/Getty Images</span>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqmref0016u9kw84dx8h82@published" data-word-count="105"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >On Monday night, struggling visibly with his coronavirus infection, Donald Trump bragged that he had triumphed over the virus. \xe2\x80\x9cI knew there\xe2\x80\x99s danger to it, but I had to do it,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump declared in a <a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/status/1313267615083761665">video</a>. \xe2\x80\x9cI stood out front. I led.\xe2\x80\x9d But the real story of Trump\xe2\x80\x99s infection is the danger he covertly posed to others. Despite multiple warning signs, he traveled to campaign events and mingled, mask-free, with donors. He knowingly jeopardized the health not just of his contributors, but of every employee who had to accompany him and everyone who had to staff these events. And he did it all for money.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--mobileOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot-mobile"\n    data-sizes="300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_m_infeedrec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqa7001c3h61vo5q8hh6@published" data-word-count="77"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >On Wednesday, Trump spoke to reporters as he left the White House for a campaign trip. The <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PG1wUzWk-4U">video</a> shows early hints of his infection. His voice was lower and more strained than it had been during a similar exchange <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tLALz2lk47Y">a few days earlier</a>. His eyes were puffy, and he sounded slightly congested. Nevertheless, he flew to Minneapolis, where he spent <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/tracking-trumps-movements-a-coronavirus-briefing-a-debate-campaign-stops-11601652398">an hour</a> talking with donors, including elderly people, at a <a href="https://www.twincities.com/2020/10/02/contact-tracing-president-trump-in-minnesota-who-hung-out-with-him-for-how-long/">$200,000-per-couple fundraiser</a> in a <a href="https://www.startribune.com/trump-s-minn-fundraiser-was-very-safely-done-guest-says/572626631/">suburban dining room</a>.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--desktopOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot"\n    data-sizes="970x250,970x90,728x90,455x256,300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "970x250,970x90,728x90,300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768486"\n    data-placement-id = "12399452"\n    data-trustx-id="3018"\n    data-criteo-id="1157134"\n    data-site-id="271363"\n    data-tl-code="slate_d_leaderboard_inline_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--tabletPortraitOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot-tablet"\n    data-sizes="728x90,300x250,455x256,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "728x90,300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768488"\n    data-placement-id = "12399457"\n    data-trustx-id="3019"\n    data-criteo-id="1157133"\n    data-site-id="271364"\n    data-tl-code="slate_d_leaderboard_inline_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <section\n You can <a href="http://link.slate.com/manage/3qk/newslettermanage">manage your newsletter subscriptions</a> at any time.</p>\n  </div>\n\n</section>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqb3001d3h61sosl7tyo@published" data-word-count="99"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >From there, Trump flew to Duluth, Minnesota, for a rally. On the way, Hope Hicks, an aide who had been physically close to the president for long periods during the week, <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-didnt-disclose-first-positive-covid-19-test-while-awaiting-a-second-test-on-thursday-11601844813">felt sick</a>. When the plane landed in Duluth, she <a href="https://www.politico.com/news/2020/10/02/trump-bubble-breach-coronavirus-positive-425531">stayed on board</a> instead of coming out for the rally. Trump, however, came out and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uYboOGy_h7E">bellowed to the crowd</a>. His voice was <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-virus-spread-white-house/2020/10/02/38c5b354-04cc-11eb-b7ed-141dd88560ea_story.html">lower and raspier</a> than when he had left the White House\xe2\x80\x94you can hear the difference in the <a href="https://www.c-span.org/video/?476320-1/president-trump-campaign-rally-duluth-minnesota">video</a>\xe2\x80\x94and his lethargy <a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-03/-top-of-his-game-the-day-covid-19-came-to-trump-s-white-house">worried some aides</a>. Instead of powering through his usual 90 minutes, he ended his speech at 45.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--mobileOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot-mobile"\n    data-sizes="300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_m_infeedrec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <div\n  data-uri="slate.com/_components/pull-quote/instances/ckfyqvm9x00253h61739y9a0a@published"\n  class="pull-quote pull-quote--left"\n  itemscope aria-hidden="true"\n>\n  <span class="pull-quote__text" data-editable="quote">Maybe Trump was trying to protect reporters from catching whatever he had. Or maybe he was just hiding<span class="widont">&nbsp;</span>symptoms.</span>\n</div>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqc9001e3h6111ef0xya@published" data-word-count="83"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >On the flight back to Washington, Hicks isolated herself, while other aides <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/10/02/us/politics/trump-positive-coronavirus-test.html">conferred</a> about her <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/10/04/us/trump-covid-symptoms-timeline.html">condition</a>. The next morning, she <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-didnt-disclose-first-positive-covid-19-test-while-awaiting-a-second-test-on-thursday-11601844813">tested positive</a> for the virus. In response, the White House did what health protocols required: It <a href="https://www.c-span.org/video/?476530-1/president-trump-experiencing-mild-covid-symptoms-white-house-chief-staff">identified aides</a> who had been physically close to her and <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-virus-spread-white-house/2020/10/02/38c5b354-04cc-11eb-b7ed-141dd88560ea_story.html">barred them</a> from a trip, scheduled for that afternoon, to a fundraiser at Trump\xe2\x80\x99s golf club in Bedminster, New Jersey. But one person who had been close to Hicks went ahead with the trip anyway: Trump himself.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--box ad--desktopOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-box"\n    data-sizes="300x250"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_dm_inline_rec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqd6001f3h610g9ar68b@published" data-word-count="90"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >According to Bloomberg News, the president was told, <a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-03/-top-of-his-game-the-day-covid-19-came-to-trump-s-white-house">before departing for the fundraiser</a>, that Hicks had tested positive. His behavior was consistent with that report. He \xe2\x80\x9csteered clear of reporters assembled for the helicopter takeoff, eschewing his normal back-and-forth and cutting an unusually wide path,\xe2\x80\x9d said the article, and he \xe2\x80\x9cavoided journalists waiting under the wing of Air Force One at Joint Base Andrews and on the flight to New Jersey.\xe2\x80\x9d Maybe Trump was trying to protect reporters from catching whatever he had. Or maybe he was just hiding symptoms.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--mobileOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot-mobile"\n    data-sizes="300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_m_infeedrec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqdx001g3h61r47bo6td@published" data-word-count="93"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >What\xe2\x80\x99s certain is that Trump, facing an expected haul of <a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-03/-top-of-his-game-the-day-covid-19-came-to-trump-s-white-house">$5 million</a>, flew to Bedminster. There, he posed for pictures with high-dollar contributors and spoke to an audience of 100 to 200 people, many of them <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-virus-spread-white-house/2020/10/02/38c5b354-04cc-11eb-b7ed-141dd88560ea_story.html">elderly</a>. He also sat and talked indoors, for more than <a href="https://www.politico.com/states/new-jersey/story/2020/10/02/trump-looked-100-percent-normal-during-bedminster-fundraiser-attendee-says-1319744">45 minutes</a>, at a <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/inside-trumps-last-public-event-before-disclosing-he-has-coronavirus-11601833568">rectangular table</a> with about 20 people who had ponied up $35,000 to $250,000 apiece. <a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-03/-top-of-his-game-the-day-covid-19-came-to-trump-s-white-house">At no point</a> did he wear a mask. According to CBS News, \xe2\x80\x9call participants were required to sign a legal waiver, agreeing <a href="https://www.cbsnews.com/news/new-jersey-contact-tracers-rnc-bedminster-frustrated/">not to sue if they contract COVID-19</a>.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqeq001h3h61y4gv0oaw@published" data-word-count="69"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >Some people who attended the fundraiser say Trump seemed tired. Others disagree. But video  recorded shortly after his return shows <a href="https://www.c-span.org/video/?476321-1/president-trump-joe-biden-speak-2020-al-smith-dinner">unmistakable congestion</a>. Sean Conley, the physician to the president, has acknowledged that on the day of the fundraiser, Trump \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.npr.org/2020/10/05/920502368/transcript-doctors-say-trump-will-continue-treatment-from-white-house">had a mild cough and some nasal congestion and fatigue</a>.\xe2\x80\x9d Conley says these \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.npr.org/2020/10/03/919894816/transcript-presidents-trumps-doctors-provide-saturday-update-on-his-health">clinical indications</a>,\xe2\x80\x9d along with Hicks\xe2\x80\x99 positive test, led White House doctors to test Trump for the virus.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--mobileOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot-mobile"\n    data-sizes="300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_m_infeedrec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--desktopOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot"\n    data-sizes="970x250,970x90,728x90,455x256,300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "970x250,970x90,728x90,300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768486"\n data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqfk001i3h617h9m5bec@published" data-word-count="126"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf" >In a <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CokeEFsGoFI">Fox News interview</a> later that evening, Trump told Sean Hannity, \xe2\x80\x9cI just went for a test. And we\xe2\x80\x99ll see what happens. I mean, who knows?\xe2\x80\x9d But Trump already knew. The test for which he was awaiting results was a PCR test, administered under White House protocols only after a positive result on the customary rapid test. According to the Wall Street Journal, Trump had <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-didnt-disclose-first-positive-covid-19-test-while-awaiting-a-second-test-on-thursday-11601844813">flunked the rapid test before the interview</a>. Comments from White House officials match that report. Trump\xe2\x80\x99s press secretary, Kayleigh McEnany, says \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://twitter.com/NBCNews/status/1312902720240717830">the first positive test he received was after his return</a>\xe2\x80\x9d from Bedminster. Conley says doctors \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.npr.org/2020/10/03/919894816/transcript-presidents-trumps-doctors-provide-saturday-update-on-his-health">repeated testing</a>\xe2\x80\x9d on Thursday afternoon. Trump\xe2\x80\x99s chief of staff, Mark Meadows, says the positive result Trump announced early Friday morning was a \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.c-span.org/video/?476530-1/president-trump-experiencing-mild-covid-symptoms-white-house-chief-staff">confirmatory test</a>.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--mobileOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n He deceived and endangered Secret Service agents, people who worked at these fundraising events, and his own aides. The Journal reports that he \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-didnt-disclose-first-positive-covid-19-test-while-awaiting-a-second-test-on-thursday-11601844813">asked one adviser not to disclose results of their own positive test</a>.\xe2\x80\x9d The president\xe2\x80\x99s exact words, according to the Journal\xe2\x80\x99s source, were: \xe2\x80\x9cDon\xe2\x80\x99t tell anyone.\xe2\x80\x9d That\xe2\x80\x99s consistent with what aides and advisers have said on the record: that despite having been in close contact with Hicks while she was infectious, they learned of her positive test <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-didnt-disclose-first-positive-covid-19-test-while-awaiting-a-second-test-on-thursday-11601844813">from media reports</a>, not from the White House. At least two of these blindsided advisers, campaign manager Bill Stepien and former New Jersey Gov. Chris Christie, have since tested positive. So has McEnany, who was sent out to brief reporters on Thursday <a href="https://slate.com/news-and-politics/2020/10/trump-press-secretary-kayleigh-mcenany-coronavirus-postive-briefing-photos.html">without a mask</a> and <a href="https://www.c-span.org/video/?476545-1/white-house-defends-presidents-decision-attend-fundraiser-aide-tested-positive">without being told</a> that Hicks\xe2\x80\x94with whom she had traveled for <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/trump-didnt-disclose-first-positive-covid-19-test-while-awaiting-a-second-test-on-thursday-11601844813">the previous two days</a>\xe2\x80\x94had tested positive.</p>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--mobileOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-spot-mobile"\n    data-sizes="300x250,1x3"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_m_infeedrec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <div data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-ad/instances/ckfyqmref0012u9kw5j6c5x87@published"\ndata-placeholder="settings"\n    class="slate-ad ad--box ad--desktopOnly ad--inArticleBanner"\n    data-type="mid-article-box"\n    data-sizes="300x250"\n    data-prebid="true"\n    data-prebid-sizes = "300x250"\n    data-zone-id = "768494"\n    data-placement-id = "12399462"\n    data-trustx-id="3020"\n    data-criteo-id="1157131"\n    data-site-id="271366"\n    data-tl-code="slate_dm_inline_rec_pb"\n>\n</div>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfyqoqhq001k3h61p6r8odb2@published" data-word-count="135"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf slate-paragraph--tombstone" >On Thursday night, when Hannity asked about Hicks\xe2\x80\x99 positive test, Trump acted as though he hadn\xe2\x80\x99t known about it before he went to Bedminster. \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CokeEFsGoFI">I just heard about this</a>,\xe2\x80\x9d said the president. And on Friday, when McEnany was asked why Trump had gone to the fundraiser despite knowing he\xe2\x80\x99d been in contact with an infected person, she said the trip was \xe2\x80\x9cdeemed safe by White House operations\xe2\x80\x9d because \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://www.c-span.org/video/?476545-1/white-house-defends-presidents-decision-attend-fundraiser-aide-tested-positive">it was an outdoor event</a>.\xe2\x80\x9d But the donors around the table in Bedminster, like those in the dining room in Minneapolis, faced the president indoors. He spoke to them at length, without a mask and without disclosing the risk that he might be infected. He cared no more about them than he did about the people who brought his food. All he cared about was the money.</p>\n\n  <p data-uri="slate.com/_components/slate-paragraph/instances/ckfzjgyvs00093h618y3wgfwb@published" data-word-count="14"\n  class="slate-paragraph slate-graf"
